Verifies qt_64 variant should exist (FAILS on buggy code)\n2. **test_qt64_uses_different_definition** - Checks qt_64 differs from qt_63 (SKIPS on buggy code)\n3. **test_variant_detection_qt64** - Confirms 6.4 falls back to qt_63 (PASSES on buggy code)\n4. **test_variant_detection_qt63** - Confirms 6.3 returns qt_63 (PASSES on buggy code)\n5. **test_threshold_setting_key_names** - Checks threshold key names (FAILS on buggy code)\n6. **test_correct_variant_routing** - Verifies variant routing is different for 6.3 vs 6.4 (FAILS on buggy code)\n\n### Test Results on Current Buggy Code\n\n```\nResults: 3 failed, 2 passed, 1 skipped\n\n✗ Bug confirmed: No qt_64 variant found\n✗ Bug confirmed: Both 6.3 and 6.4 use TextBrightnessThreshold  \n✗ Bug confirmed: 6.4 and 6.3 both use qt_63 variant\n```\n\nThe test can be run with:\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null --timeout=60 /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```","stop_reason":null,"session_id":"bb9b551c-e495-4740-b956-a27832c60d1a","total_cost_usd":0.34958610000000007,"usage":{"input_tokens":310,"cache_creation_input_tokens":54246,"cache_read_input_tokens":1560356,"output_tokens":20305,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":54246,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"modelUsage":{"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001":{"inputTokens":19043,"outputTokens":21340,"cacheReadInputTokens":1560356,"cacheCreationInputTokens":54246,"webSearchRequests":0,"costUSD":0.34958610000000007,"contextWindow":200000,"maxOutputTokens":32000}},"permission_denials":[],"uuid":"e08e12f7-3650-428d-badc-cbc9d2daf668"}
